Texas Street. Shreveport, La	1907	Postcard : color ; 3 x 5 in.	Caption on back: 'Texas Street. This broad and elegant thoroughfare is the main business section of Shreveport, and here scenes of active life are evidenced at all times, furnishing a strong index to the progressive spirit of its citizens. At its western elevated terminal is the First Methodist Church, while fronting it are the Government Building, the Court House, Serwich and Phoenix Hotels, Merchants and Farmers Bank and many imposing business structures.'
